GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_p*sin(c2*A)

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: -0.10017·√A + 0.47149·sin(0.85551·A)**

This is a function of A only (no t dependence). The GT has two basis functions: √A and sin(linear in A).

Let me analyze each candidate systematically. For a candidate to match, it must:
1. Be reducible to a function of A only (all t-dependent terms must be eliminable)
2. Contain the basis functions √A and sin(linear in A), or equivalent forms

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2/(A^c1 + c3) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
- Set c4=0 to kill t-dependence. Remaining: `A*c0 + A^c1*c2/(A^c1+c3) + c6`
- This gives polynomial/rational functions of A. No sin or √A that can't be absorbed. The term A^c1*c2/(A^c1+c3) is a saturating function, not sin. Cannot produce sin(A).
- Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `A²c0 + A²c1 + Ac2 + Ac3/(Ac4+1) + A^c5·c6 + c7·exp(c8t) + c9/A⁵`
- Set c7=0. Remaining terms are rational/power functions of A. No sin term.
- Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `A*c0*exp(c1/(c2+c3*t)) + c4*tanh(c5*t+c6) + c7*|A|/(c8*|A|+1)`
- To eliminate t: need c3=0 in exp term (making it constant), and c5=0 in tanh (making it constant). Then: `A*c0*exp(c1/c2) + c4*tanh(c6) + c7*A/(c8*A+1)` (using A≥0). No sin or √A.
